        "import keras\n",
        "from keras.preprocessing import image\n",
        "from keras.engine import Layer\n",
        "from keras.layers import Conv2D, UpSampling2D, InputLayer, Conv2DTranspose, Input, Reshape, merge, concatenate\n",

        "from keras.callbacks import TensorBoard \n",
        "from keras.models import Sequential, Model\n",

        "from keras.preprocessing.image import ImageDataGenerator, array_to_img, img_to_array, load_img\n",
        "from skimage.color import rgb2lab, lab2rgb, rgb2gray, gray2rgb\n",
        "from skimage.transform import resize\n",
        "from skimage.io import imsave\n",

      "cell_type": "code",

        "id": "jxft77mlV7te"
      },
      "source": [
        "def preprocess(image):\n",
        "  X = rgb2lab(1.0/255*image)[:,:,0]\n",
        "  Y = rgb2lab(1.0/255*image)[:,:,1:]\n",
        "  Y /= 128\n",
        "  X = X.reshape(1, 256, 256, 1)\n",
        "  Y = Y.reshape(1, 256, 256, 2)\n",
        "  return X, Y"
      ],
      "execution_count": 11,
      "outputs": []
    },
    {
      "cell_type": "code",
      "metadata": {
        "id": "_xDqkYoVVnEX"
      },
      "source": [
        "X_files = []\n",
        "Y_files = []\n",
        "\n",
        "for file_name in os.listdir('drive/MyDrive/colorImages/ColorizerImages'):\n",
        "  image = img_to_array(load_img(os.path.join('drive', 'MyDrive', 'colorImages', 'ColorizerImages', file_name)))\n",
        "  image = np.array(image, dtype=float)\n",
        "  image = tf.image.resize(image, [256,256])\n",
        "  X,Y = preprocess(image)\n",
        "  X_files.append(X)\n",
        "  Y_files.append(Y)\n",
        "\n",
        "X_files = np.asarray(X_files)\n",
        "Y_files = np.asarray(Y_files)\n",
        "\n",
        "#image = img_to_array(load_img(\"drive/MyDrive/grassfield.jpg\"))\n",
        "#image = np.array(image, dtype=float)\n",
        "#image = tf.image.resize(image, [256,256])\n",
        "\n"

      "source": [
        "model = Sequential()\n",
        "InputLayer(input_shape=(256, 256, 1,))\n",
        "model.add(Conv2D(32, (3, 3), activation='relu', padding='same', strides=2))\n",
        "model.add(Conv2D(64, (3, 3), activation='relu', padding='same'))\n",
        "model.add(Conv2D(64, (3, 3), activation='relu', padding='same', strides=2))\n",
        "model.add(Conv2D(128, (3, 3), activation='relu', padding='same'))\n",
        "model.add(Conv2D(128, (3, 3), activation='relu', padding='same', strides=2))\n",
        "model.add(Conv2D(256, (3, 3), activation='relu', padding='same'))\n",
        "model.add(Conv2D(256, (3, 3), activation='relu', padding='same'))\n",
        "model.add(Conv2D(128, (3, 3), activation='relu', padding='same'))\n",
        "\n",
        "model.add(Conv2D(64, (3, 3), activation='relu', padding='same'))\n",
        "model.add(UpSampling2D((2, 2)))\n",
        "model.add(Conv2D(32, (3, 3), activation='relu', padding='same'))\n",
        "model.add(UpSampling2D((2, 2)))\n",
        "model.add(Conv2D(16, (3, 3), activation='relu', padding='same'))\n",
        "model.add(Conv2D(8, (3, 3), activation='relu', padding='same'))\n",
        "model.add(Conv2D(2, (3, 3), activation='tanh', padding='same'))\n",
        "model.add(UpSampling2D((2, 2)))"
      ],
      "execution_count": 16,
      "outputs": []
